










































































































SELECT cchat.id, cchat.from, cchat.to, cchat.message,
 cchat.sent, cchat.read, cchat.type, cchat.status, u.id AS userid, sess.session_id AS loggedin, u.username AS fromuser
 FROM #__jchat AS cchat
 INNER JOIN #__session AS sess ON cchat.from = sess.session_id
 LEFT JOIN #__users AS u ON sess.userid = u.id
 WHERE (cchat.to = '432d4932ee8ea9b33a96c5ec4b0b8f58' AND cchat.read != 1)
 ORDER BY cchat.id

 ORDER BY cchat.id
